*Reincarnation*, *Mutate*, *MutateGaia*, *Attach*, *Spawn* and *Root*.

\- ***freezeType*:** OnHitEffect freeze effect type. Only applicable
for *Freeze*. Valid values are *default* (freeze type used by Frost
Giant attack), *stone* (petrification with instant death behavior for
Legacy AoM), *stoneDamage* (new petrification behavior of Medusa and
Perseus special attacks), *acid* (Argus special attack behavior for
Legacy AoM) and *sand.*- ***damage*:** Damage to be applied for
onHitEffect. Only applicable for *Freeze* onHitEffect with
*stoneDamage freezeType*.

\- ***amount*:** Unit amount to be spawned through a *Spawn*
onHitEffect.

\- ***attachBone*:** Target attach bone for *Attach* onHitEffects.

\- ***shadingType*:** OnHitEffect shading type. Only applicable for
*ProgShading*, *ShadingFade* and *Shading* onHitEffects.

\- ***fadeTime*:** OnHitEffect fade time for target shading change.
Only applicable for *ShadingFade* onHitEffects.

\- ***factor*:** Target factor for onHitEffect shading change. Only
applicable for *Shading* and *ShadingFade* onHitEffects.

\- ***anim*:** Animation. Only applicable for *AnimOverride*
onHitEffects.

\- ***protoAction*:** Infection protoAction. Only applicable for
*Infect* onHitEffects.

\- ***hideVFX:*** Does not spawn default Stun VFX when set to
'*true*'. Only applicable for *Stun* onHitEffects

Beyond that, additional data can be assigned to an onHitEffect through
the following child nodes.

\- ***Modify*:** Assigns a modifier towards a particular modify type
to this onHitEffect. Only applicable for *StatModify*, *Boost* and
*SelfModify* onHitEffects. Takes the following parameters:

31

• ***type*:** Modify type for modifier\
• ***dmgType*:** Damage type for *ArmorSpecific* and *DamageSpecific*
modify types. • ***applyType*:** Modifier apply type. Can be set to
*set*, *add* or *multiply*. Defaults to *multiply*. Not applicable to
all modify types.

• ***stack*:** If present, modifier will be allowed stack, allowing it
to be applied more than once at the same time.

\<OnHitEffect type=\'StatModify\' duration=\'5.000000\'\>

\<Modify type=\'ROF\'\>2.000000\</Modify\>

\<Modify type=\'Speed\'\>0.500000\</Modify\>

\</OnHitEffect\>

\- ***ModifyRamp*:** Assigns a modifier towards a particular modify
type to this onHitEffect, with a rate that, during the duration of the
effect, varies linearly from a defined initial value to a final value.
Takes the same attributes as *Modify*, plus the following: •
***init*:** Defines initial value for modifier.

• ***final*:** Defines final value for modifier.

\<OnHitEffect type=\'Boost\' duration=\'5.000000\'
radius=\'10.000000\'\>

\<ModifyRamp type=\'Speed\' init=\'1.500000\' final=\'1.000000\' /\>

\<ModifyRamp type=\'Damage\' init=\'1.500000\' final=\'1.000000\' /\>

\</OnHitEffect\>\
- ***Target*:** Sets valid or restricted target data for a provided
OnHitEffect. Unlike\
*targetUnitType* parameter, though, does not allow multiple
OnHitEffects towards the same type to be defined if set to have
distinct target data. Takes either of the following parameters:\
• ***AttackType*:** Defines a valid target type for the onHitEffect.

• ***IgnoreType*:** Defines a restricted target type for the
onHitEffect.

\<OnHitEffect type=\'Attach\' proto=\'VFXPoison\'
duration=\'5.000000\'\>

\<Target AttackType=\'Unit\' /\>

\<Target IgnoreType=\'AbstractTitan\' /\>

\</OnHitEffect\>\
- ***Damage*:** Defines per-type damage data for a *DamageOverTime*
onHitEffect, that will account for protoAction damage bonuses and
target unit's armor. Takes one parameter, *type*, which sets the
intended damage type.

\<OnHitEffect type=\'DamageOverTime\' duration=\'1.000000\'\>

\<Damage type=\'Pierce\'\>30.000000\</Damage\>

\<Damage type=\'Divine\'\>8.000000\</Damage\>

\</OnHitEffect\>\
● **Charged:** Sets up a charged modifier data for a ProtoAction,
which can be activated under defined conditions. Takes the following
attributes as children nodes:\
- ***ChargedModify*:** Sets core modify data. Takes the following
attributes:\
• ***modifyType*:** Sets modify type.

• ***param*:** Sets damage type for *ArmorSpecific* and *DamageSpecific*
modify types.

• ***applyType*:** Sets apply type for modifier. Can be set to *set*,
*add* or *multiply*. Defaults to *multiply*. Not applicable to all
modify types.

• ***modifyAmountCap*:** Sets limit for maximum modify rate for this
modifier, in cases where modifiers can be altered either through
action-based stacking (e.g. handling done for *StackControl*
protoActions) or through age-based bonuses.

\<Charged\>

32

\<ChargedModify modifytype=\'LifeSteal\'
applytype=\'Set\'\>0.8\</ChargedModify\>

\<Duration\>10\</Duration\>

\<Cooldown\>0\</Cooldown\>

\<ActivationType\>KillEnemy\</ActivationType\>

\</Charged\>\
- ***ChargedModifyAgeBonus*:** Sets age-based bonuses for this
modifier. Takes the following parameters:\
• ***age*:** Age in which this modifier bonus entry will be applied.

• ***applyType*:** Apply type for this modifier bonus entry. Can be
set to *set*, *add* or *multiply*. Does not replace apply type for the
modifier, but only determines how the current modify bonus entry will
alter the modifier value, once active.

\<Charged\>

\<ChargedModify modifytype=\'Armor\'
applytype=\'Multiply\'\>1.0\</ChargedModify\>

\<ChargedModifyAgeBonus age=\'ClassicalAge\'
applytype=\'Add\'\>0.1\</ChargedModifyAgeBonus\>

\<ChargedModifyAgeBonus age=\'HeroicAge\'
applytype=\'Add\'\>0.2\</ChargedModifyAgeBonus\>

\<ChargedModifyAgeBonus age=\'MythicAge\'
applytype=\'Add\'\>0.3\</ChargedModifyAgeBonus\>

\<ChargedModifyAgeBonus age=\'WonderAge\'
applytype=\'Add\'\>0.3\</ChargedModifyAgeBonus\>

\<ChargedModifyVFX\>VFXOpportuneTime\</ChargedModifyVFX\>

\<ActivationType\>Combat\</ActivationType\>

\<Duration\>5.0\</Duration\>

\<Cooldown\>40.0\</Cooldown\>

\</Charged\>\
- ***ChargedRemove*:** If set to 'true', causes the last instantiated
*ChargedModify* action to be removed upon activation. Used for stack
depletion actions within stackable effect management (i.e. as used by
Taotie).

\- ***ChargedModifyVFX*:** VFX protoUnit to be spawned upon modifier
activation.

\- ***ChargedModifyVFXDuration*:** VFX duration in seconds.

\- ***HitpointsRatioThreshold*:** Hitpoint threshold below which
modifier will be activated if *ActivationType* is set to
*BelowHitpointsThreshold*.

\- ***Stealth*:** If present, unit will enter stealth mode upon
modifier activation.

\- ***ActivationType*:** Determines which event triggers modifier
activation. Can be set to *Combat* (activated by combat start),
*BelowHitpointsThreshold* (activated if unit is below a given hitpoint
ration), *AfterAction* (activated after completion of a particular
action), *KillEnemy* (activated after killing an enemy unit),
*UseByAbility* (activated when manually cast), *UseOnce*
(single-usage), *TerrainType* (activated when unit is over a provided
terrain type), *Always* (always active, as long as protoAction is
Active),\
*ChargedActionActive* and *AuxChargedActionActive* (reliant on
recharge state for main and auxiliary charges, respectively).

\- ~~***VFXActivationType*:** Unused and deprecated.~~

\- ***Cooldown*:** Charged modify cooldown in seconds.

\- ***Duration*:** Charged modify duration in seconds.

\- ***SetTactic*:** Tactic to be set once modifier is activated.

\- ***TerrainType*:** Terrain type for modifier activation, when
*ActivationType* is set to *TerrainType*. Can be set to *Water* or
*Land*.

\- ***ChargedModelAttachment*:** Animfile path for charged modifier
attachment.

\- ***ChargedModelAttachmentBone*:** Bone for charged modifier
attachment.

● **StackControl:** Defines stackable bonus/effect handling data for a
*StackControl* protoAction. Takes the following parameters, defined as
child nodes:\
- ***StackMax*:** Maximum amount of times effects from the protoAction
defined in

33

*StackAddAction* can be applied over the unit and *StackSubAction* can
be cast/used. - ***StackAddAction*:** ProtoAction that applies actual
stacakble bonuses/effects.

\- ***StackSubAction*:** ProtoAction that can be used once per stacked
bonus/effect. Depletes one bonus/effect stack per usage.

● **TrailProtoUnit:** Sets trail data for *Trail* protoActions or VFX
data for *IdleStatBonus* protoActions. Takes one attribute,
*frequency*, which defines the time interval in which the proto unit
is spawned while the unit is performing movement for *Trail*
protoActions or the number of tiers/levels for VFX spawning for
*IdleStatBonus* protoActions.

\<TrailProtoUnit frequency=\'0.25\'\>FeiTrail\</TrailProtoUnit\>

**Flags**\
● **AttackAction:** Sets protoAction as a valid attack action.

● **Active:** Sets protoAction as active.

● **ActiveIfContainsUnits:** Causes protoAction to be actually active
only while units are garrisoned. Only functional for attack actions,
and *AutoConvert*, *AutoGather*, *AutoRangedModify*, *Maintain*,
*ModifyGather* and *Spawn* protoActions.

● **ScaleByContainedUnits:** Scales attack according to the amount of
garrisoned units. Shouldn't be set if protoAction is supposed to use
*ScaleByContainedUnitType*.

● **HandLogic:** Defines protoAction as a hand attack action.

● **RangedLogic:** Defines protoAction as a ranged attack action.

● **SpeedBoost:** Causes unit speed to be boosted by a predefined
factor upon attacking. ● **TargetSpeedBoost:** Causes target unit
speed to be hindered by a predefined factor upon attacking.

● **Persistent:** Causes protoAction to be persistently processed.

● **AddResourcesToInventory:** If set, *AutoGather* action will
deposit resources within unit's inventory, instead of the player's
stockpile.

● **AddResourcesFasterWhenOwned:** If set, *AutoGather* actions will
generate resources 25% faster wen owned by a non-Nature/Gaia player;\
● **SingleUse:** Causes protoAction to be useable only once. Only
valid for *AutoGather*, *Build*, *Maintain*, *Spawn* and *Attaching*.

● **SingleUsePlayer:** For *Spawn*, causes protoAction to be
effectively deactivated, preventing other instances of this unit from
using it.

● ~~**Throw:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **InitialROF:** Requires unit to reload before performing the first
attack.

● **Linear:** For *Maintain* actions, causes the number of produced
units to be incremented by one at each iteration. The maximum number
of units that can be produced in a iteration is capped by the work
rate value.

● **NoCost:** Causes manually set *AutoRepair* protoActions to not
cost resources.

● **BaseDamageCap:** Causes area attack actions to not account for
damage bonuses for damage cap checking.

● **DropsiteGathering:** Enables dropsite gathering for gathering
actions.

● **TargetGround:** Causes ranged actions to use the ground position
of the unit as a reference for targeting.

● **InstantBallistics:** Causes projectiles to travel instantly,
instead of at their movement

34

speed.

● **SelfDestruct:** Causes unit to self-destruct upon attacking.

● **PerfectAccuracy:** Causes ranged attack to be fully accurate on
non-moving targets. ● **ChargeAction:** Sets this protoAction as a
charged attack action.

● **ShowQueueWhileWaiting:** If set, *Maintain* actions will be shown
in both the unit queue and the global game queue, if they are on
waiting state. Set to 1 by default.

● **HideFromGlobalQueue:** If set, *Maintain* actions will not be
shown in the global game queue but will appear in the unit queue. Set
to 0 by default.

● **DoNotAutoGatherUnlessGathering:** If set, it will cause the
*AutoGather* action to not generate resources if unit isn't performing
a gathering action.

● **TargetEnemy:** Causes an *AutoRangedModify* or *AreaMutate*action
to affect only enemy units. ● **TargetNature:** Causes an
*AutoRangedModify* or *AreaMutate*action to affect only nature units.

● **ModifyExclusive:** Causes other *AutoRangedModify* actions sharing
the same modifyType to not be processed.

● **ExcludeFromRangeIndicator:** Excludes action from being processed
for range decal displaying.

● ~~**CastWhenAnimationFinished:** Deprecated.~~

● **TargetGaia:** Causes an *AutoRangedModify* action to affect only
Gaia units.

● **DoNotIgnoreDead:** Causes an *AutoRangedModify* action to also
affect dead units. For *Maintain* actions, include dead units in the
*ModifyTargetLimit* count.

● **DeadExclusive:** Restrict an *AutoRangedModify* action to only
affect dead units.

● **SingleUnit:** Causes an *AutoRangedModify* action to only affect a
single target.

● **IncludeNature:** Causes an *AutoRangedModify* action to affect
Gaia units, besides of player units.

● **HideFromStats:** Hides protoAction from unit stats.

● **ForceUpdateMode:** Forces units affected by an AutoRangedModify
action set to not persistently update (i.e. with the *StartOnNoUpdate*
protoUnit flag set) to full update state, allowing them to be properly
affected by auras.

● **ModifySelf:** Causes *AutoRangedModify* and *LikeBonus* actions to
affect the source unit. ● **AuxChargeAction:** Sets this protoAction
as a secondary charged attack action.

● **CannotBeConvertedByAllies:** Prevents an *AutoConvert* action from
causing a friendly player from capturing the unit.

● **TargetUnbuilt:** Restricts an *AutoRangedModify* action to only
affect targets which aren't fully built (i.e. building foundations and
buildings under construction).

● **TargetEnemyIncludeNature:** Causes an *AutoRangedModify* action to
affect only enemy or gaia units.

● **NoStack:** Prevents more than one instance of an
*AutoRangedModify* action of the same source unit from affecting the
same target unit, while still allowing it to be affected by other
*AutoRangedModify* actions set to the same modifyType.

● **SquareAura:** Causes the area of effect of an *AutoRangedModify*
action to be a square, instead of circular.

● **GatherLinkedResource:** Causes an *AutoGather* action to consume
socketed resources to generate resources.

● ~~**DontKillWhenExpired:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **RestrictToGatherers:** Restricts an *AutoRangedModify* action to
only affect units gathering

35

from the source unit.

● **HealNonIdle:** Allows a *Heal* action to heal units which wouldn't
receive full heal rate (i.e.

units that aren't idle, nor are performing gathering, healing or
building, or that have been attacked or performed any attack on the
last 3s). Set by default.

● **IncludeAlly:** Causes an *AutoRangedModify* action to affect
allied units, besides of player units.

● **ModifyRateByType:** Causes a *LikeBonus* protoAction to have
inverted aura behaviour, making nearby units within the area defined
by *MaxRange* of the unitType defined in *ModifyAbstractType* to
contribute to the bonus applied to the source unit by rates defined
through the *WorkRate* entries.

● **ModifySingleActionByType:** Causes *AutoRangedModifyAction* to not
target an unit if it's already affected by another action set to the
same *ModifyType*.

● **NoStackIgnorePUID:** When set alongside with *NoStack*, also
prevents instances of the protoAction from other protoUnits from
affecting the same target unit.

● **AutoGatherScaleByGatherRate:** Causes *AutoGather* rate to be
affected by the current gather rate of the unit.

● **SpawnIgnoreBuildLimit:** Causes a *Spawn* action to spawn units,
regardless of build limit. ● ~~**HandAttackDisplayRange:** Unused and
deprecated.~~

● **AttachForceDieWithUnit:** When in an *Attaching* action, causes an
unit without lifespan set attached to an enemy unit to be forcibly
removed once the unit dies.

● ~~**DisableAutoAttack:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **RestrictToIdleUnits:** Restricts an *AutoRangedModify* action to
only affect units that are currently idle.

● **RestrictToValidRepairTargets:** Restricts an *AutoRangedModify*
action to only affect units that are valid targets for the Repair
command.

● **KeepAlive:** Forces a single-use *Maintain* or *Spawn* action to
be kept alive, internally, preventing it from being re-triggered, in
case persistent actions are reloaded through tactic switching. For an
*AreaMutate* protoaction, maintains the effect as long as the source
protounit is alive.

● **ModifyRangeUseLOS:** Causes an *AutoRangedModify* action to use
the current unit's LOS as its effective range.

● **AttachValidTargetOnly:** Causes *AttachProtoUnits* to only be
spawned when the attack action has properly targeted a living valid
target.

● **SpawnOnAnimationLoop:** For *Spawn* protoActions,causes spawning
to be performed once the current unit animation ends.

● **DestroyUnitAfterUse:** For *Spawn* protoActions, causes source
unit to be killed after spawning action is performed when used
alongside with the *SpawnOnAnimationLoop* protoAction flag.

● **ModifySelfOnly:** Restricts an *AutoRangedModify* protoAction to
only affect the current unit.

● **AutoGatherTeam:** For *AutoGather* actions, causes the resource
trickle to benefit all players within the team, instead of just the
owner of the unit.

● **CannotBeConvertedByEnemies:** Prevents an *AutoConvert* action
from causing an enemy player to capture the unit.

● **ForceSpawn:** Forces a *Spawn* action to be processed, and
executed if/when applicable, by the game, in case it's assigned to a
starting unit or building.

36

● **ConvertToNatureIfForbidden:** For *AutoConvert* actions, causes
unit to be converted to Nature/Gaia, in case it's captured by a player
who has been forbidden from capturing the current unit through
scenario or RM triggers.

● **IncludeEnemy:** For inverted aura actions (*LikeBonus* with
*ModifyRateByType* flag set), causes valid Enemy units to be accounted
for modifier calculation.

● **Pausable:** Allows a *Maintain* action to be paused by
right-clicking over it on in-game HUD. Set by default.

● **IncludeUnbuilt:** Allows an *AutoRangedModify* action to affect
targets which aren't fully built (i.e. building foundations and
buildings under construction), without explicitly restricting to
those.

● **KillOnTrain:** For *Maintain* protoActions, causes unit to be
killed once unit generation is complete.

● **RestrictIfEmpowered:** Restricts an *AutoRangedModify* action to
only affect units that are currently being empowered.

● **WorkOnStoneUnits:** Allows an attack action to target units that
have been petrified through Legacy petrification effect.

● **WorkOnFrozenUnits:** Allows an attack action to target units that
have been frozen. Set by default.

● **CircularShockwave:** Causes *BuckAttack* protoAction to perform a
circular shockwave around the unit's position.

● **LinearShockwave:** Causes *BuckAttack* protoAction to perform a
linear shockwave (e.g. similar to Centimanus special attack) on the
direction of the unit's attack.

● **HomingBallistics:** Causes fired projectiles to perfectly follow
target unit in its trajectory.

● **PassThrough:** Causes fired projectile to pass through multiple
targets until reaching maximum action range, damaging any units it
passes through, while stopping when reaching a building.

● ~~**AttackBoost:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **ShockStun:** If set, *StunAttack* events will be sent to attack
action when dealing damage. Only applicable for *Gore* actions.

● **AreaDamageIgnoreType:** Causes area damage to affect units
regardless on whether or not the protoAction has valid rates towards
them.

● **ForceAreaAttackTarget:** Forces an attack action set to have a
range lesser than 1 to perform area attack using target position as
reference for damage propagation.

● **DefaultAttack:** Sets action as the default attack to be displayed
on in-game UI stats panel. ● **ContainScaleBaseDamage:** Seems to
double damage of the protoUnit?

● **ModifyFlyingUnits:** For *AutoRangedModify* actions, allows flying
units to be affected.

● **SendUnderAttackEvent:** *For AutoRangedModify* actions that
perform progressive damage, causes under attack events to be sent to
affected units, ensuring that run away behavior is properly handled.

● **TargetNonAlly:** Restricts an *AutoRangedModify* action to only
affect units belonging to players that are not allied with unit owner
(including Neutral players).

● **FullDamageMainTarget:** For attack actions set to perform area
damage, full damage is dealt to main target, regardless its distance
to area damage epicenter.

● **Exclusive:** Restricts action to only be used towards units that
aren't already being targeted or otherwise affected by an instance of
this action.

37

● **PassThroughBuildings:** Causes fired projectile to pass through
multiple targets, including buildings, until reaching maximum action
range, damaging any units it passes through. ●
**ForceAreaAttackCenter:** Forces an attack action set to have a range
greater than or equal to 1 to perform area attack using attacker
position as reference for damage\
propagation.

● **PreDamageAction:** Causes onHitEffects to be applied before actual
damage is dealt.

● **CharmedConvert:** Enables charmed conversion behavior for
*Convert* actions.

● **SuspendByAttack:** Sets an *AutoRangedModify* action to be
suspended while attack is being performed.

● **FaceToAfterTeleport:** For *TeleportAttack* protoActions, causes
unit to face its target after teleporting to it.

● **BackToAfterTeleport:** For *TeleportAttack* protoActions, causes
unit to face the opposite direction to its target after teleporting to
it.

● **OnlyAnimMove:** For *DelayedTransform* actions, prevents actual
position change from being done during transform sequence, if unit is
to perform taking off from a landed state into a flying state or
vice-versa.

● **MustFinishAnimation:** For *DelayedTransform* actions, prevents it
from being cancelled/interrupted by player commands.

● ~~**TerrainAnimVariation:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **AreaDamageIgnoreTacticAttackType:** Causes area damage to affect
units regardless on whether or not they are regarded as valid targets
by Tactic data.

● **AttachAboveUnit:** Causes attachment for an *AutoRangedModify*
action to be placed above the unit if bone is set to
*bonethatdoesntexist*.

● **AutoCastBySelf:** Allows actions set as charged actions, but which
do not or cannot take an explicit enemy target, to be auto-activated
if the unit has the *CastAbilitySelf* protoUnit flag set.

● **NotSuspendByAttack:** For *IdleStatBonus* protoActions, causes
rate increase to not be halted while unit is performing an attack, if
its position has not changed.

● **AutoRetarget:** For attack actions that have multiple *attack*
events defined within attack animation, allows attack sequence to
continue by locating a new target, if it's main target has died before
attack sequence is complete.

● **CanAttackGround:** For attack actions with *AutoRetarget* flag
set, allows attack to be directed at ground, if no new targets have
been found.

● **ModifyAttachOnce:** For *AutoRangedModify* action, prevents
attachment from being attached to the unit more than once, if it
happens to be affected by multiple instances of that protoAction.

● **ModifySelfIfInfection:** Causes an *AutoRangedModify* action to
affect the unit it's assigned to, if it has been assigned through an
infection effect.

● **DoNotAutoGatherIfGathered:** Prevents an *AutoGather* protoAction
from generating resources, if unit has been gathered.

● **ProgressiveYield:** For *AutoGather* protoActions, causes resource
generation rate to linearly grow from its base amount (defined through
a *MinRate* entry) to its final amount (defined in the *Rate* entry
for the given resource) through the time defined in seconds through
the *yield* attribute.

● **RestrictToWater:** Restrict the protoaction to be used only in
water.

38

● **AllyDamageMultiplier:** Defines the damage multiplier for allied
units affected by the protoaction.

● **ModifyInventoryScale:** For *LikeBonus* actions, modify the
amount/multiplier according to the percentage of resources left in the
inventory of the protounit.

**Modify Types**\
● **Speed:** Unit maximum speed.

● **MaxHP:** Unit maximum hit points.

● **Damage:** Unit damage. Affects all damage types.

● ~~**MovingDamage:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **SiegeDamage:** Unit siege damage. Affects, specifically, the
damage inflicted against buildings and ships, and not necessarily all
protoActions with the damageType set to *Siege*. ● **Bounty:** Kill
bounty obtained by affected units.

● **UnitDamage:** Damage inflicted against units (as in non-buildings
and non-ships).

● **LOS:** Line of Sight. Increases unit's LOS linearly, rather than
in a multiplicative manner. ● **Armor:** Unit armor. Affects all
damage types.

● **GatherRate:** Gather rate for all resources.

● **AbilityROF:** Ability cooldown time for power set in
*ModifyProtoPower*. Does not affect abilities with global cooldown or
using charging time.

● **ROF:** Unit rate of fire.

● **AutoGatherRate:** AutoGather rate for all actions.

● **UnitResource:** Consumes resource inventory for natural resources
at a linear rate, based on the *ModifyAmount* attribute value.

● **BaseHP:** Unit hit points, applied over base protoUnit hitpoints,
instead of the current value. ● **BuildingWorkRate:** Building Work
Rate.

● **BuildRate:** Affects Building construction rate when affecting
builders. Affects auto-building rate when affecting foundations placed
by wagons.

● **Chaos:** Enables Chaos behaviour on affected units.

● **FarmingGatherRate:** Gather rate for farm objects (*AbstractFarm*
unitType).

● **InfluenceRate:** Rate in which resources gathered by affected
units will be converted into Influence.

● **HealRate:** Linear heal rate, or progressive damage, if set as a
negative value. For buildings, hit points addition/subtraction will be
percentage-based.

● **AutoGatherAbsolute:** AutoGather rate for all actions with a rate
greater than zero. Adds to the AutoGather rate linearly, instead of
multiplying.

● **RepairCost:** Building repair cost.

● **TrainingRate:** Building unit training rate.

● **EconomicTrainingRate:** Building economic unit training rate.

● **MilitaryTrainingRate:** Building military unit training rate.

● **ResearchRate:** Building technology researching rate.

● **ResourceGatherRate:** Resource gathering rate multiplier for
gatherers gathering from the affected unit.

● **ResourceYield:** Resource yield rate multiplier for gatherers
gathering from the affected unit.

39

● **NaturalFoodGatherRate:** Gather rate for natural food sources
(targets with Food as their main resource and either *Nature* or
*NatureClass* types set).

● **TreeGatherRate:** Gather rate for trees.

● **MineGatherRate:** Gather rate for mines (*MinedResource*
unitType).

● **AutoBuildRate:** Auto-building rate for foundations placed by
wagons.

● **PeaceFlag:** Causes affected units to be perceived as friendly
units by enemies, preventing them from being attacked by enemy units
and vice-versa.

● **BaseDamage:** Unit damage, applied over base protoUnit damage,
instead of the current value.

● **BuildBounty:** Building build bounty. Does not affect resources
other than XP.

● **RechargeTime:** Charged action recharge time. Affects both main
and auxiliary recharge times.

● **Range:** Maximum range.

● **RangeAbsolute:** Maximum range. Adds linearly, instead of
multiplying.

● **Shield:** Redirects damage received by targeted units by the rate
defined in\
*ModifyMultiplier*. For units affected by multiple *Shield* auras,
redirected damage is split between aura sources.

● **FavorGatherRate:** Unit AutoGather rate for Favor.

● **DropsiteRate:** Multiplier applied over resources deposited at
this unit.

● **DoubleTrainChance:** Chance of spawning an additional unit after
successful training. ● **GodPowerBlockRadius**: Radius in which unit
will cause God Power casting to be blocked.

● **AuraEmpower:** Propagates empowering effects defined in
ProtoAction data towards all units affected by the aura.

● **MilitaryTrainingCost:** Training cost for military units from this
unit.

● **DamageSpecific:** Type-specific damage. Damage type is defined by
the *ModifyDamageType* protoAction attribute.

● **ArmorSpecific:** Type-specific armor. Damage type is defined by
the *ModifyDamageType* protoAction attribute.

● **AutoGatherFactor:** Factor by which total AutoGather rate for this
unit will be divided by.

● **NumProjectiles:** Number of projectiles fired by ranged attack
actions. Adds to base number of projectiles linearly, instead of in a
multiplicative manner.

● **VisualScale:** Unit visual scale.

● **ProgFreezeSpeed:** Rate by which unit's movement speed is lowered.

● **LOSFactor:** Line of Sight. Increases unit's LOS in a
multiplicative manner, rather than linearly.

● **ForcedTarget:** Causes affected units to become uncontrollable and
forcibly attack aura source unit.

● **RevealUI:** Reveals in-game UI and queue for this unit to source
player of the aura. ● **MaxShieldPoints:** Unit shield points.

● **ShieldRegenRate:** Regeneration rate for shield.

● **BaseShieldPoints:** Unit shield points, applied over base
protoUnit shield, instead of the current value.

● **GatherRateMultiplier:** Unit gather rate multiplier applied over
total collected resources. ● **Invulnerable:** Causes affected units
to be invulnerable to attacks.

● **LifeSteal:** Dynamic rate for lifesteal effect, causing hitpoints
of affected units to be restored 40

by a rate of total inflicted damage against a target.

● **DecaySpeed:** Resource decay speed for dead animals.

● **TradeRate:** Multiplier applied over total trade income for this
unit.

● **DodgeChance:** Chance for the unit to dodge an attack.

● **ConstructionSuspended:** Halts construction and repair progress
for affected buildings. ● **CommandResearchCost:** ProtoUnitCommand
research cost from this unit.

● **RegenRate:** Unit regeneration rate defined through protoUnit or
civilization data. ● **InventoryAmount:** ProtoUnit resource inventory
amount.

● **InventoryExtraCap:** ProtoUnit resource inventory maximum carry
capacity.

41

**OnHitEffect Types**\
● **Stun:** Stuns target unit for the defined duration.

● **StatModify:** Applies the modifiers defined within OnHitEffect
data for the provided duration. Modifiers applied by the same
ProtoAction do not stack.

● **Snare:** Ensnares the target unit by the provided duration,
modifying its speed by the value provided in the *rate* attribute.
Snare effects do not stack: when a unit is affected by multiple snare
effects, the one with the lowest multiplier will be prioritized.

● **DamageOverTime:** Applies damage over time for target unit,
according to the damage values provided in the *Damage* children nodes
or through the *rate* parameter, for the provided duration. Damage
defines through the *rate* parameter does not account for damage
bonuses or target armor.

● **Lifesteal:** Restores hitPoints for attacker by the percentage
defined in *rate* of the total amount of damge inflicted against the
target unit.

● **Reincarnation:** Causes target unit to transform into the
protoUnit provided through the *proto* attribute and be converted to
attacking player, if it dies during the duration of the effect.

● **Throw:** Throws target units. Throwing-related ProtoAction
attributes override default hardcoded parameters whenever applicable\
● **Freeze:** Applies freezing effect for the effect duration,
according to the type provided through the *freezeType* attribute.

● **Boost:** Applies modifiers defined within OnHitEffect data for all
player-owned units belonging to the unitType defined through
*targetUnitType* within the radius defined in the *radius* attribute.
Modifiers applied by the same ProtoAction do not stack.

● **Push:** Pushes the target unit by the force provided through the
*radius* parameter.

● **Mutate:** Mutates/transforms target unit into protoUnit defined in
the *proto* attribute.

● **MutateGaia:** Mutates/transforms target unit into protoUnit
defined in the *proto* attribute, converting it to Nature/Gaia.

● **Attach:** Attaches the protoUnit defined in the *proto* attribute.
Effect duration determines the lifespan of the object to be attached.

● **Pull:** Pulls the target unit towards the attacker by the force
provided through the *radius* parameter.

● **Spawn:** Spawns the protoUnit defined in the *proto* attribute by
the amount defined in the *amount* attribute. If set, Effect duration
determines the lifespan of the spawned objects. ● **ProgFreezeSpeed:**
Progressively slows the target by the rate defined on the *rate*
attribute each attack, causing it to be frozen when reaching 0 speed,
by the duration provided in the *freezeDuration* attribute.

● **Chaos:** Causes target unit to remain uncontrollable and attack
the closest unit for the provided druation.

● **SelfModify:** Applies modifiers defined within OnHitEffect data to
the attacker.

● **ProgFreezeROF:** Progressively slows the target attack speed by
increasing its ROF by the rate defined on the *rate* attribute each
attack, causing it to be frozen as soon as its attack becomes 2X
slower than its base attack, by the duration provided in the
*freezeDuration* attribute.

42

● **ProgShading:** Sets shading type to be applied for progressive
movement speed/ROF reduction to the type defined by the *shadingType*
attribute. As the target unit's speed/ROF is reduced by
*ProgFreezeSpeed* or *ProgFreezeROF* effects, the factor for the
provided shading type will be adjusted accordingly.

● **ShadingFade:** Applies a temporary shader to the target for the
defined duration. Fading time for the shader is defined by the
*fadeTime* attribute.

● **TreeFlatten:** Flattens a target tree using the same effect as
used by the *Implode* god power.

● **AnimOverride:** Overrides target animation by the animation
provided through the *anim* attribute for the provided duration.

● **Shading:** Permanently applies the shading type provided through
the *shadingType* parameter with the factor provided through the
*factor* parameter.

● **Exile:** Causes target to become invisible during the duration of
the effect.

● **Root:** Progressively slows the target by the rate defined on the
*rate* attribute, while spawning and attaching the protoUnit defined
on the *proto* attribute. Once the target's movement speed reaches
zero, ensures it remains locked in place for the standard duration of
the effect.

● **Flee:** Causes target to flee from attacker and remain
uncontrollable for the duration of the effect.

● **Infect:** Assigns the AutoRangedModify protoAction defined through
the *protoAction* to target for the given duration, while ensuring
that, after assigned, affects units owned by the target unit's owner.

● **SelfStealth**: makes the unit enter stealth mode.

**Tactic Data**\
● **Active:** Defines whether the tactic is active or not. Set to 1
(Active) by default.

● **Action:** Adds a valid action for this tactic. Takes either of two
attributes, *priority*, which defines choice priority for attack
actions, or *probability*, which sets the chance percentage (as an
integer from 0 to 100) of the given action to be activated by the unit
when performing an attack.

● **SpeedModifier:** Modifier to be applied to unit movement speed
after switching to the current tactic.

● **MaxHPModifier:** Modifier to be applied to unit hitpoints after
switching to the current tactic.

● **DamageModifier:** Modifier to be applied to unit damage after
switching to the current tactic.

● **UnitDamageModifier:** Modifier to be applied to unit damage
against living targets (as in non-buildings and non-ships) after
switching to the current tactic.

● **AttackType:** Unit type that defines valid attack targets. Tactics
support multiple *AttackType* nodes.

● **ExcludeAttackType:** Restricted unit type for attack targets.
Tactics support multiple Exclude*AttackType* nodes.

● **AutoAttackType:** Unit type that defines valid auto-attack
targets. If not set, auto-attack will be disabled for the current
tactic.

● **AttackResponseType:** Unit type that defines valid retaliation
targets.

● **AttackMoveType:** Valid attack type for targeting while performing
attack move.

43

● **RunAway:** If set, enables running away behaviour.

● **AutoRetarget:** If set, units will look for other targets
automatically, if current attack target becomes invalid\
● **AgeRequirement:** Minimum age required for this tactic to be
available. Set as an integer value. Not handled by in-game UI.

● **AbilityOnly:** If set, tactic won't be activable or togglable by
any means other than abilities or charged modifiers.

● ~~**Transition:** Not applicable for AoM: Retold.~~

● **IdleAnim:** Idle animation for current tactic.

● **BoredAnim:** Bored animation for current tactic.

● **DeathAnim:** Death animation for current tactic.

● **WalkAnim:** Movement animation for current tactic.

● **MoveAnim:** Movement animation for current tactic.

● ~~**JogAnim:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **RunAnim:** Running animation for current tactic.

● **ArmorOverride:** Armor override value to be used when this tactic
is set. Takes two attributes, *type* and *value*, which define,
respectively, the armor type and armor value for the override.
Requires *UseTacticArmorOverride* protoUnit flag to be set for proper
functionality. When using this system, separate armor values will need
to be defined for each tactic.

● **AttackPriorityType:** Denotes a unit type which will receive an
additional bonus attack prioritization factor when this tactic is
active. Takes one attribute, *bonusFactor*, which defines the bonus
value to be added to the attack prioritization factor.

\<AttackPriorityType
bonusFactor=\'50.00\'\>MythUnit\</AttackPriorityType\>

44

**ProtoUnitCommands (proto_unit_commands.xml)**

**Attributes**\
● **Name:** ProtoUnitCommand internal name.

● **Command:** Console command to be executed.

● **Icon:** ProtoUnitCommand icon path.

● ~~**ActiveIcon:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● ~~**DisabledIcon:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **AssociatedTech:** Technology associated with the protoUnitCommand,
defining command availability, cost and research time.

● **TrainableUnitReq:** Restricts the availability of this command on
whether or not the given protoUnit is available for the current
player.

● **PrereqCommand:** Binds the availability of this command on the
previous execution of the given protoUnitCommand.

● **DisplayNameID:** String ID for protoUnitCommand displayed name.

● **RolloverTextID:** String ID for default protoUnitCommand rollover.

● **ShortRolloverTextID:** String ID for shortened protoUnitCommand
rollover.

● **ActiveRolloverTextID:** For ProtoUnitCommands linked to Building
Tactics, defines the rollover to be displayed when the tactic is
currently active.

● **DisabledRolloverTextID:** String ID for protoUnitCommand rollover
to be displayed when command cannot be currently issued, despite it's
being currently shown.

● **BuildLimitTextID:** String ID for protoUnitCommand build limit
notification, for transform commands.

● **ValueText:** Value text to be displayed over protoUnitCommand
icon.

● **AssociatedPower:** Associates the protoUnitCommand with the given
protoPower, causing it to share cooldown with the protoPower.

● **ForbidTech:** Technology to be temporarily forbidden while this
protoUnitCommand is being researched, if it's associated with a
technology.

● **ProtoUnit:** ProtoUnit to be spawned, if *SpawnCommand* is set.

● **Amount:** Amount of units to be spawned, if *SpawnCommand* is set.

● **CostProtoUnit:** Sets protoUnit whose cost will be shown as
command cost. For researchable protoUnitCommands, effectively
overrides cost obtained from associated tech.

● **Age:** Age in which protoUnitCommand is intended to be made
available.

● **SharedCommand:** Sets a protoUnitCommand as a shared command,
allowing it to be researched for selected units that have it assigned
within their data, if the source command has the *ResearchOnSelected*
flag set and has been activated.

**Flags**\
● **CommandPassesUnitID:** If present, first integer printf parameter on
command will be replaced by the internal ID of the current unit.

● **UseMultiple:** If present in a protoUnitCommand associated with a
particular technology, it will allow the protoUnitCommand to be
executed multiple times.

45

● **DoNotAllowOverPopLimit:** Forbids the command from being executed
if player is above the population limit.

● **DoNotAllowIfUnitDamaged:** Forbids the command from being executed
if current unit is damaged.

● **RequireUnitDamaged:** Forbids the command from being used if
current unit is not damaged.

● ~~**BindToChargeAction:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **SpawnCommand:** Causes protoUnitCommand to spawn units once
executed. Requires the protoUnitCommand to be associated with a
technology for proper functionality.

● ~~**CastPower:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **SocketBuild:** If present, indicates that the current
protoUnitCommand triggers a SocketBuild command, and causes it to
display the cost, if applicable.

● ~~**DisplayAsPassive:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **NotCancellable:** If present, protoUnitCommand, if researchable,
won't be cancellable once queued.

● **Deploy:** If present, denotes that this protoUnitCommand will
perform a deployment action for a building which uses deployment
ungarrisoning.

● **SiteBasedCommand:** Sets protoUnitCommand as a site-based command,
allowing it to be visible within in-game UI even if selected unit is
not within LOS, to be displayed and usable in some cases for units not
owned by the current player, and hidden from UI if site-based commands
are disabled through game settings.

● **AllowedOnOtherPlayers:** Allow this command to be displayed and
executable for other players in a Nature/Gaia-owned object.

● **Transform:** If present, performs a transformation command,
without performing checks for or relying on *TransformCommand*
protoUnit attribute, or explicitly propagating the command to all
selected units.

● **TransformSelected:** If present, when executed with multiple units
selected, triggers the respective *TransformCommand*, if applicable,
for each selected unit, excluding units belonging to the
*AbstractVillager* unitType.

● **TransformVillager:** If present, when executed with multiple units
selected, triggers the respective *TransformCommand*, if applicable,
for each selected unit belonging to the *AbstractVillager* unitType.

● **UnitCommand:** If present, command will display blue frame on
in-game UI around its icon, rather than black neutral border/frame.

● **DisplayOnTarget:** For transform commands, allows it to be
displayed on UI if the main selected unit is a transformation target
and at least one among the selected units can be transformed through
this command or through commands set through the\
*TransformCommand* attribute.

● **ResearchOnSelected:** If present, when researching this command
with multiple units selected, causes the same command (or commands set
to be shared) to be researched through all selected units when
applicable.

● **Reusable:** If present, allows a command that requires
research/use tracking for proper handling (e.g. transform commands) to
be re-usable over the same unit ID in some circumstances.

46

● **SharedCommandHotkey:** If set, shared command data will be
accounted for when querying for the hotkey for this command.

47

**Civilization/Major God Data (major_gods.xml)**

**Attributes**\
● **Name:** Internal Civilization name.

● **Main:** Denotes whether the civilization is meant to be a playable
civilization, when set to 1, or a SubCiv/Revolution civilization,
otherwise.

● ~~**StatsID:** Deprecated.~~

● **Culture:** Civilization culture, as defined in culture data in
cultures.xml.

● **Key:** Key to be used for fetching correct display string for
units using rollovers with civilization-specific text.

● **DisplayNameID:** String ID for civilization/major god displayed
name.

● **RolloverNameID:** String ID for civilization/major god rollover.

● **TitleID:** String ID for civilization/major god title, displayed
in major god selection UI. ● **Icon:** Major god/civilization icon
path, relative to *game\\ui_myth*.

● **Portrait:** Major god/civilization portrait path, relative to
*game\\ui_myth*.

● **BreakoutPortrait:** Major god/civilization icon breakout portrait
path, used in major god selection UI, relative to *game\\ui_myth*.

● **MinimapBorderImage:** Major god/civilization minimap border
texture path, relative to *game\\art*.

● **BackgroundScenario:** Major god/civilization background scenario
path, to be displayed on main menu background after playing as this
major god/civilization, relative to\
*game\\campaign*.

● **AgeTech:** Assigns a technology, through a child *Tech* node, to
be activated once the player reaches a given age, set through an *age*
parameter.

\<AgeTech age=\"ArchaicAge\"\>

\<Tech\>ArchaicAgeFuxi\</Tech\>

\</AgeTech\>\
● **DeathMatchTech:** Technology to be activated when in DeathMatch
game mode.

● **TeamTech:** Technology to be activated for all team players at the
beginning of the game, akin to AoE2 Team Bonuses. Multiple instances
of the same civilization or the same technology don't cause its effect
to stack.

● ~~**EmpireWarsTech:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **BuildingEfficiency:** Work rate multiplier to be applied to the
second builder on foundations.

● **ExtraBuildingEfficiency:** Work rate multiplier for additional
builders on foundations. ● **BuildingRepairFactor:** Building repair
cost factor. Defaults to 0.5 if not set.

● **StartingUnits:** Sets up starting units for a given game mode for
this major god/civilization.

Takes one parameter, *mode*, which defines the game mode the units
will be assigned to (can be set to *supremacy*, *deathmatch* and
*lightning*; defaults to *supremacy*; game modes with no specific
starting unit data set default to using *supremacy* data). Each
starting unit entry is defined through *Unit* child nodes, which can
take up the following attributes: - ***count*:** Unit count for
starting unit entry\
- ***delay*:** Starting unit spawning delay in seconds.

\- ***x*:** Position offset on the X axis for unit movement upon
spawning.

48

\- ***y*:** Position offset on the Y axis for unit movement upon
spawning.

\- ***z*:** Position offset on the Z axis for unit movement upon
spawning.

\- ***resourceAmount*:** Initial resource amount for spawned starting
units. Requires protoUnit to support resource storage by default.

\<StartingUnits mode=\'deathmatch\'\>

\<Unit count=\'9\' delay=\'2\' x=\'0.00\' y=\'0.00\'
z=\'0.00\'\>VillagerGreek\</Unit\>

\<Unit count=\'1\' delay=\'4\' x=\'-12.00\' y=\'0.00\'
z=\'0.00\'\>Kataskopos\</Unit\>

\</StartingUnits\>

● **StartingResources:** Sets up starting resources for a given game
mode for this major god/civilization. Takes one parameter, *mode*,
which defines the game mode the provided starting resources will be
assigned to, handled in the same way as it is for *StartingUnits*.
Starting amount for a given resource is defined through a child node.

\<StartingResources\>

\<Food\>200\</Food\>

\<Wood\>250\</Wood\>

\<Gold\>50\</Gold\>

\</StartingResources\>

● **StartingQueue:** Sets up starting queue for the player's initial
Town Center for a given game mode for this major god/civilization.
Takes one parameter, *mode*, which defines the game mode the provided
starting queue data will be assigned to, handled in the same way as it
is for *StartingUnits*. Each queue entry is defined through a *Unit*
entry, which can take the following parameters:\
- ***autoTrain*:** Enables auto-queue for the given protoUnit when set
to 'true', if applicable. - ***preQueue*:** Adds given protoUnit to
prequeue when set to 'true', if applicable.

\- ***count*:** Amount of units to be queue. Not applicable if either
*autoTrain* or *preQueue* are set.

\- ***delay*:** Queue delay in milliseconds.

\<StartingQueue mode=\'deathmatch\'\>

\<Unit autotrain=\'true\'\>VillagerGreek\</Unit\>

\<Unit prequeue=\'true\'\>Jason\</Unit\>

\</StartingQueue\>

● **TerrainCreeps:** Sets up terrain creep data, which defines terrain
modification data for buildings (e.g. as used for Gaia Lush handling).
Terrain creep entries are defined through *TerrainCreep* children
nodes, valid protoUnits for terrain creep spreading are assigned
through *ProtoUnit* subchildren nodes. *TerrainCreep* nodes can take
the following attributes: - ***creep*:** Terrain reep type, as defined
in *terrain_creep_types.xml*.

\- ***maxRadius*:** Maximum expansion radius out of a single building.

\- ***growthRate*:** Terrain creep radius growth rate per game second.

\- ***decayRate*:** Terrain creep radius decay rate per game second
after a building gets destroyed.

49

\- ***strength*:** Terrain creep strength. When expanding terrain
creep to a terrain tile already taken by another terrain creep type,
the terrain creep type with higher strength takes priority.

\- ***minUpdateInterval*:** Minimum update interval in seconds for
terrain creep expansion update.

\- ***maxUpdateInterval*:** Maximum update interval in seconds for
terrain creep expansion update.

\- ***avoidUnbuildable*:** If present, terrain creep won't expand to
unbuildable tiles.

\- ***avoidImpassable*:** If present, terrain creep won't expand to
impassable tiles.

\- ***avoidShallowWater*:** If present, terrain creep won't expand to
shallow water tiles. - ***allowDisconnectedGrowth*:** If present,
terrain creep will be able to expand to tiles not directly adjacent to
tiles already overtaken by terrain creep.

\- ***buildability*:** Defines whether or not tiles overtaken by this
terrain creep type will be unbuildable. Can take one of the following
values: *buildable* (buildable by all players), *unbuildable*
(unbuildable by all players), *unbuildableSelf* (unbuildable by
owner), *unbuildableOthers* (unbuildable by players other than owner),
*unbuildableAllies* (unbuildable by allied players, including owner),
*unbuildableEnemies* (unbuildable by enemy players).

\<TerrainCreeps\>

\<TerrainCreep creep=\"GaiaCreep\" maxRadius=\"24.0\"
growthRate=\"0.50\"

decayRate=\"0.5\" minUpdateInterval=\"3.0\" maxUpdateInterval=\"4.0\"

avoidUnbuildable=\"\" avoidImpassable=\"\"\>

\<ProtoUnit\>TownCenter\</ProtoUnit\>

\<ProtoUnit\>VillageCenter\</ProtoUnit\>

\<ProtoUnit\>CitadelCenter\</ProtoUnit\>

\<ProtoUnit\>Manor\</ProtoUnit\>

\<ProtoUnit\>EconomicGuild\</ProtoUnit\>

\<ProtoUnit\>Market\</ProtoUnit\>

\</TerrainCreep\>

\</TerrainCreeps\>

● **Partisans:** If set, enables the spawning of partisan units upon
building destruction, if set in protoUnit data.

● **Shades:** If set, sets up data for spawning units upon the death
of a particular unit type at one of the player's temples, as used by
the Hades Shade mechanic. Takes the following attributes, defined as
child nodes:\
- ***ProtoUnit*:** ProtoUnit to be spawned upon death of valid units.

\- ***TargetUnit*:** Defines a valid unit type for triggering spawning
upon death. Multiple *TargetUnit* children nodes can be set.

\- ***Chance*:** Chance of triggering spawn upon death, set as a
floating-point value between 0 and 1.

\- ***Delay*:** Spawning delay in seconds.

\<Shades\>

\<ProtoUnit\>HadesShade\</ProtoUnit\>

\<TargetUnit\>HumanSoldier\</TargetUnit\>

50

\<Chance\>0.2\</Chance\>

\<Delay\>10.0\</Delay\>

\</Shades\>

● **BonusUnitSpawning:** Sets data for goal-based unit spawning.
Mechanic can be set as enabled or disabled by default according to the
value of an *Active* child node. Multiple goals can be assigned, which
are defined through children nodes, setting the goal type (i.e.

events that contribute to or trigger unit spawning):\
- ***DamageGoal*:** Sets up a damage-based goal, causing units will be
spawned, based on the total damage inflicted by unit types defined
within goal data.

\- ***DeathCountGoal*:** Sets up a goal based on units lost by the
player, causing units to be spawned according to the total amount of
units lost belonging to given types defined within goal data.

\- ***ResourceGoal*:** Sets up a goal based on resource gathering,
causing units to be spawned based on the total amounts of resources
gathered of types defined within goal data.

Each goal can take the following inline attributes:\
- ***name*:** Internal goal name, to be used for indexing and for
modifying goal data through technology effects.

\- ***rewardTracking*:** Sets how reward progress will be tracked for
unit spawning. Can be set to either *Single* (reward progress is
unified, and all damage done or units lost by/of valid unit types
contribute to the progress of next unit to be spawned, which is
randomly picked), or *PerPossibleReward* (progress is tracked
separately for each potential spawning reward, and damage done or
units lost by/of valid unit types only contribute for the spawning of
units belonging of the same protoUnit). *Resource* goals only support
*Single* reward tracking type.

The following additional data can be assigned to a goal as children
nodes:\
- ***Reward*:** UnitType for potential spawn rewards. Multiple
*Reward* nodes can be assigned to a single goal.

\- ***Contributor*:** Defines valid unit types (for *Damage* and
*DeathCount* goals) or gatherable resource types (for *Resource*
goals) for reward progress and their contribution rates, which
determines how much each obtained reward point from either that unit
type or that resource actually contribute to reward progress. Takes
either a *unit* or *type* parameter (for *Damage* and *DeathCount*
goals, or a *resource* parameter (for *Resource* goals).

\<Contributor type=\'HumanSoldier\'\>0.1\</Contributor\>

\<Contributor resource=\'Favor\'\>1.0\</Contributor\>\
- ***GoalAmount*:** Determines how much damage (for *Damage* goal),
lost units (for *DeathCount* goal) or resources gathered (for
*Resource* goal) is needed for progressing 1 reward point for the next
spawn.

\- ***ExcludeFromReward*:** UnitType to be excluded from potential
spawn rewards. Multiple nodes can be assigned to a single goal.

\- ***ExcludedTarget*:** For *Damage* goals, defines target unitTypes
that do not contribute to reward progress when dealing damage against.

51

\- ***SpawnLocation*:** Defines where granted spawn rewards will be
spawned. Takes the following attributes:\
• ***type*:** Defines the spawning target type. Can be set to
*DamageTarget* (spawns unit at target of the last damage that
contributed to reward points), *DamageDealer* (spawns unit at last
attacker that contributed to reward points), and *FromBuilding*
(spawns unit at a building belonging to a given unitType). The first
two are only applicable for *Damage* goals.

• ***landBuilding*:** If *type* is set to *FromBuilding*, defines
building unitType where land- based spawn rewards will be spawned.

• ***waterBuilding*:** If *type* is set to *FromBuilding*, defines
building unitType where water- based spawn rewards will be spawned.

\<SpawnLocation type=\'FromBuilding\' landBuilding=\'Temple\'
waterBuilding=\'Dock\' /\\<SpawnLocation type=\'DamageTarget\' /\>

\- ***RewardPointCost*:** Defines the rate in which the cost for a
particular resource for a given unitType will contribute to the total
reward points required to spawn that unit, once it's selected as a
reward. Takes one parameter, *resourceType*, which sets the resource
type.

\<RewardPointCost resourceType=\'Food\'\>1.0\</RewardPointCost\>

\- ***Active*:** Defines whether goal is active or not.

\- ***ForceSpawn*:** If set, selected reward will be spawned once
enough reward points are obtained, even if current population cap
would be exceeded.

\- ***AgeRestricted*:** If set, units made available in later ages
will be able to be selected as potential spawn rewards.

\- ***CultureRestricted*:** If set, only units belonging to the
player's culture will be selected as potential spawn rewards.

\- ***ArchaicSpawn*:** If set, any valid units for spawn reward
selection made available within Archaic age will be considered as so,
instead of being grouped together alongside Classical Age units.

\- ***CurrentAgeOnly*:** If set, spawn reward will be selected among
units available within the current age.

\- ***NextAgeOnly*:** If set, spawn reward will be selected among
units available within the next age.

\- ***IgnoreAgeRoll*:** If set, potential spawn rewards will be
selected among units available within the first age in all cases.

\- ***DisplayOnHUD*:** If set, goal progress will be displayed on
in-game HUD, according to data set within *DisplayInfo* node. Only
applicable for *Resource* goals.

\- ***DisplayInfo*:** Sets data for in-game HUD goal progress
indicator, if *DisplayOnHUD* flag is set for a *Resource* goal. Takes
the following parameters as children nodes:\
• ***DisplayNameID*:** String ID for displayed title for HUD goal
progress indicator tooltip. • ***RolloverID*:** String ID for rollover
for HUD goal progress indicator tooltip.

52

• ***ProgressTooltipID*:** String ID for formatted progress string for
HUD goal progress indicator tooltip.

• ***NextUnitTooltipID*:** String ID for formatted string listing next
unit to be spawned for HUD goal progress indicator tooltip.

• ***ProgressType*:** Progress bar type. Can be set to *Default* (same
color as age-up circular progress bar), *ShieldBlessing* (blue
circular progress bar) or *SpawnReward* (green circular progress bar).

• ***Icon*:** HUD goal progress indicator icon, relative to
*game\\ui_myth*\\resources*.*

• ***NotificationSound*:** Sound to be played when a unit is
successfully spawned. • ***NotificationMessageID*:** Formatted
notification message to be displayed when a unit is successfully
spawned.

● **BountyResourceEarning:** Sets data for resource generation based
on damage dealt or units killed. Takes the following parameters as
children nodes:\
- ***Active*:** Sets whether the mechanic is to be active or not.

\- ***ExcludedTarget*:** Adds a unitType to be excluded from resource
generation when dealing damage against or destroying.

\- ***BountyDamageGoal*:** Amount of total damage to be inflicted in
order to earn the full resource reward for damage defined for the
current attacker through *BountyReward* data.

\- ***BountyReductionStart*:** When generating Favor, determines how
much resources need to be collected for generation rate to be reduced.

\- ***BountyReductionEnd*:** When generating Favor, determines how
much resources need to be collected for the maximum reduction rate
defined through the\
*BountyReductionStrength* attribute to be applied.

\- ***BountyReductionStrength*:** When generating Favor, determines
the maximum reduction rate to be applied over generated resources when
the amount of generated Favor reaches *BountyReductionEnd*. The
reduction rate to be applied grows linearly once generating the amount
of favor defined in *BountyReductionStart* up until reaching the
maximum value.

\- ***BountyReward*:** Defines resource generation data for a
particular unitType. Takes the following attributes:\
• ***unitType*:** Reference UnitType for this entry.

• ***protoUnit*:** Reference UnitType for this entry.

• ***resourceType*:** Resource type for this entry. For CombatXP,
replaced by combatxp="".

• ***condition*:** Resource generation condition. Can be set do
*Damage* or *Destroy*. When set to *Damage*, defines how much
resources of the provided resource type units of the aforementioned
unitType will generate once total damage dealt by them reaches the
value set on *BountyDamageGoal*. When set to *Destroy*, determines how
much resources will be obtained when destroying an enemy unit
belonging to the\
aforementioned unitType.

\<BountyReward unitType=\'Ship\' condition=\'Damage\'

resourceType=\'Favor\'\>0.5\</BountyReward\>

53

\<BountyReward unitType=\'House\' resourceType=\'Wood\'

condition=\'Destroy\'\>25.0\</BountyReward\>

\- ***BountyTargetMultiplier*:** Defines multiplier to be applied over
resources obtained from dealing damage against a particular unitType.
Takes the following parameters: • ***unitType*:** Target UnitType this
multiplier is intended to be applied to.

• ***protoUnit*:** Target UnitType this multiplier is intended to be
applied to.

• ***resourceType*:** Resource type to be affected by multiplier.

• ***condition*:** Should be always set to *Damage*, as this is not
applicable to on-destroy resource generation.

\<BountyTargetMultiplier unitType=\'Building\' condition=\'Damage\'

resourceType=\'Favor\'\>0.1\</BountyTargetMultiplier\>

\- ***ResearchReward*:** Defines resource generation data for a
research type. Takes the following attributes:

• ***techType*:** Reference techType for this entry.

• ***resourceType:*** Resource type for this entry. For *CombatXP*,
replaced by combatxp="".

\- ***ResearchCostMultiplier:*** Defines multiplier to be applied over
the resource cost of the researched tech. Takes the following
parameters:

• ***techType*:** Reference techType for this multiplier.

• ***resourceType*:** Resource type for this multiplier.

\- ***excludedTechFlag:*** Tech to be excluded from ResearchReward.

\- ***VFX*:** VFX protoUnit to be spawned when generating resources
either through dealing damage or destroying valid targets.

● **TimeShifting:** Sets data for time shifting mechanic. Takes one
parameter,\
*maxConcurrentTimeShifts*, which defines the maximum amount of
buildings that can be timeshifted at a time. Valid time shifting
targets are defined by *ProtoUnit* children nodes, which take the
following parameters:\
- ***costRatio*:** Time shifting cost ratio according to building's
cost.

\- ***timeRatio*:** Time shifting duration ratio according to
building's build points.

\<TimeShifting maxConcurrentTimeShifts=\'1\'\>

\<ProtoUnit costRatio=\'0.0\' timeRatio=\'0.50\'\>Manor\</ProtoUnit\>

\<ProtoUnit costRatio=\'0.50\'
timeRatio=\'0.667\'\>Palace\</ProtoUnit\>

\</TimeShifting\>

● **BuildingChain:** Sets data for building chain mechanic, as used
for Chinese culture favor generation. Takes the following children
nodes:\
- ***Anchor*:** Sets a unitType for triggering chain resource
generation logic: any building connected to a building that belongs to
a unit type set as *Anchor*, either directly or indirectly, will be
considered as part of the chain and will generate resources. Takes one
parameter, *vfx*, which sets the VFX protoUnit to be displayed once an
anchor building is selected.

\<Anchor vfx=\'VFXFavorGlow\'\>AbstractSocketedTownCenter\</Anchor\>

54

\- ***ChainableBuilding*:** Defines a valid building for building
chain. Takes two parameters, *chainRadius*, which defines the radius
for linking/connecting this building with other buildings, and
*generationResource*, which defines the resource that will be
generated by tiles covered by this building once linked to an anchor
building.

\<ChainableBuilding generationResource=\'Favor\'

chainRadius=\'20.0\'\>TownCenter\</ChainableBuilding\>

\- ***ResourceGeneration*:** Defines tiered resource generation rate
data for building chain system. Each tier is defined by a
*TileRatePerMinuteTier* child one, which sets the resource generation
rate per tile per tier, and can take the following parameters •
***resource*:** Resource type for resource generation.

• ***minTiles*:** Minimum amount of tiles for the provided per-tile
resource generation rate to be used for tiles covered by buildings
linked to an anchor building.

\<ResourceGeneration\>

\<TileRatePerMinuteTier resource=\'Favor\'
minTiles=\'0\'\>0.0125\</TileRatePerMinuteTier\>

\<TileRatePerMinuteTier resource=\'Favor\'
minTiles=\'750\'\>0.01\</TileRatePerMinuteTier\>

\</ResourceGeneration\>

\- ***AbundanceVFX*:** Sets VFX data for Abundance effect, defining
the protoUnits for VFX to be spawned when depositing resources over
dropsites affected by Abundance effect (i.e. *DropsiteRate*
modification applied for dropsites within Building Chain*)*. Takes
three attributes, *small*, *medium* and *large* to be spawned for
buildings with obstruction radius over the X axis lesser than or equal
to 2, greater than 2, or greater than or equal to 5, respectively.

\<AbundanceVFX small=\'VFXAbundanceSmall\'
medium=\'VFXAbundanceMedium\'

large=\'VFXAbundanceLarge\' /\>\
- ***AutoBuildVFX*:** Sets VFX data for Auto-Build effect, defining
the protoUnits for VFX to be spawned foundations being auto-build
within Building Chain radius. Takes three attributes, *small*,
*medium* and *large* to be spawned for buildings with obstruction
radius over the X axis lesser than or equal to 2, greater than 2, or
greater than or equal to 5, respectively.

*\<AutoBuildVFX small=\'VFXAutoBuild\' medium=\'VFXAutoBuild\'*

*large=\'VFXAutoBuild\'/\>*

● **CombatXP:** defines the amount of combat XP needed to reach the
different tiers. Effects are defined in the Powers file through a
SwitchingEffects protopower.

\<combatxp\>

\<tier\>1\</tier\>

\<tier\>2000\</tier\>

\</combatxp\>

**Non-Civilization Attributes**\
● **DefaultPopLimit:** Default base population limit.

● **DefaultContainedRegenRate:** Default percentage-based regeneration
rate for garrisoned

55

units within buildings.

● **DefaultRepairFactor:** Default repair cost factor to be used if no
valid building repair factor is set within civilization data.

● **LightningTech:** Global technology to be applied when in Lightning
game mode, regardless of selected civilization.

● **DeathMatchTech:** Global technology to be applied when in Death
Match game mode, regardless of selected civilization.

● **StoryModeTech:** Technology to be applied for human player when
playing a Campaign scenario in Story Mode.

● **LudicrousModeTech:** Technology to be applied for AI players when
playing a Campaign scenario in Ludicrous Mode.

● **DeathMatchPowerGrantDelay:** Defines the delay in milliseconds
before the first usage of a granted God Power is available in Death
Match mode for each age. Takes children nodes set to the internal age
names for defining the delay for a given age.

\<DeathMatchPowerGrantDelay\>

\<ArchaicAge\>80\</ArchaicAge\>

\<ClassicalAge\>140\</ClassicalAge\>

\<HeroicAge\>200\</HeroicAge\>

\<MythicAge\>260\</MythicAge\>

\</DeathMatchPowerGrantDelay\>

56

**TechTree (techtree.xml) Core Data**\
**Attributes**\
● **DisplayNameID:** String ID for the technology displayed name.

● **Cost:** Technology cost. Takes one parameter, *resourcetype*,
which sets the resource type for each entry.

● **ResearchPoints:** Total amount of time in seconds required to
research the technology. ● **ResearchLimit:** Number of times in which
the technology can be researched. Set to 1 by default.

● **Status:** Initial availability status of the technology. Can be
set to *UNOBTAINABLE*, *OBTAINABLE* or *ACTIVE*.

● **TechType:** Assigns a technology type. Valid technology types are
defined in *game\\data\\gameplay\\tech_types.xml*.

● **Icon:** WPF path for technology icon, relative to *game\\ui_myth*.

● **RolloverTextID:** String ID for the technology long rollover.

● **AdvancedRolloverTextOverrideID:** String ID for advanced effect
rollover override.

● **ValueText:** Value text to be displayed over technologies, akin to
the ones used in protoUnitCommands. Supports the same data fetchers as
the ones supported by protoUnitCommands. Requires the technology flag
*DEUsesValueText* to be set for proper functionality.

● **Delay:** Delay for applying technology effects in seconds, as soon
as tech status is set or toggled into active. Only applicable for
auto-activable techs.

● **InitialDelay:** Delay for applying technology effects in seconds
for first tech activation, as soon as tech status is set or toggled
into active. Only applicable for auto-activable techs. ● **TechAge:**
Age to be used for activating this tech for Scenario starting age
logic.

● **CombatXPTier:** CombatXP tiers linked to this tech, for Japanese's
Bushido for example.

**Flags**\
● **Volatile:** Denotes a technology that's meant to be automatically
activated once its prerequisites are met.

● ~~**AlwaysShowButton:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● ~~**ExcludeFromPlaytest:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **DynamicCost:** Causes the technology cost to scale according to
the number of enemy units present on the map.

● **AgeUpgrade:** Denotes a technology to be used for minor god
selection.

● **HideFromDialogs:** If set, technology won't be listed in advanced
rollovers, nor over available and applied research listings in in-game
help dialogues.

● **HideAllNotifications:** Denotes technologies that aren't supposed
to be counted for the total numbers of researches of a player, nor be
shown in the UI or generating notifications or effect text upon
research.

● ~~**UpgradeTech:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **TeamTech:** Causes the effect of the technology to be applied to
the entire team of the player who researched it.

57

● **OrPrereqs:** Causes the prerequisites of a technology to be
processed using *OR* logic, allowing the technology to be made
available as soon as at least one of the tech prerequisites are met.

● **CountsTowardEconomicScore:** Causes the technology to count toward
economic score once researched.

● **CountsTowardMilitaryScore:** Causes the technology to count toward
military score once researched.

● **DoNotQueue:** Allows the technology to override and ignore the
building queue to be researched.

● **InfiniteTech:** Self-explanatory.

● ~~**AlwaysDisableButtonInGrid:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **ForceUnapply:** Forces the technology to be reverted once it's set
to *Unobtainable* status. ● **NoTextMessage:** Causes the technology
to not generate notifications upon research, but

still be able to display text through text output effects and be counted
among a player's

researched technologies.

● **UsesValueText:** Allows a technology to display value text.

● **DoNotAllowDuringNoRush:** Forbids a technology from being
researched while Ceasefire is active.

● **HideAdvancedRollover:** Causes advanced effect information to not
be shown for the technology.

● **Reversible:** For technologies with the *Volatile* flag set,
ensures their effects are reverted once their prereqs are no longer
met, while allowing them to be re-activated once their prereqs are
once again met.

● ~~**ForceCostUpdate:** Unused and deprecated.~~

● **PlayerTechCostAbsolute:** Used for *TechCostAbsolute* data effect
logic.

● **DESetObtainableIfFailed:** If set, technology will become
obtainable and re-researchable, in case its effects have failed to be
applied.

● **Persistent:** For technologies with the *Volatile* flag set, after
their prereqs are no longer met, allow them to be re-applied when
their prereqs return to a met state.

● **AgeTech:** Denotes a technology that holds generic/general effects
to be applied for a given culture or major god, when reaching a
specific age, regardless of the chosen minor god. ● **MythTech:** If
set, technology will display purple border of mythical upgrades.

● **Titans:** If set, technology will not be available if 'Allow
Titans' is set to be disabled within lobby settings.

● **DelayedFirstActivation:** If set, delay will be accounted for the
first activation of this tech. ● **ExcludeFromKBCostTracking:** If
set, technology won't be accounted for KB tracking of a player's total
research cost.

● **IgnoreIfAutoActivated:** If set, this technology won't be
accounted for *OnTechResearchedTech* handling if it has been
auto-activated.

● **MultipleActivation:** For technologies with the *Volatile* and
*Persistent* flags set, once the technology has no longer its prereqs
met, allows it to be reactivated multiple times, while obeying any
delays set within technology data, until the technology prereqs are
once again met.

58

● **NeverAutoResearch:** Prevents technology from being
auto-researched if its\
researchPoints are set to zero, or when setting a player's starting
age to an age higher than the one it's made available in.

● **IgnoreForUIAgeAvailabity:** Causes this technology to be ignored
for the logic used to determine the age in which units or technologies
are meant to be available.

● **IgnoreForPreloading:** Causes this technology to be ignored for
determining which unit assets need to be preloaded.

● **ForceUnapplyIfActive:** Forces the technology to be reverted once
it's set to *Unobtainable* status, if and only if its previous state
was *Active*.

59

+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+
|             |             | **r       | Defines   |             |
|             |             | elativity** | how the   |             |
|             |             |             |           |             |
|             |             |             |  attribute\ |             |
|             |             |             | should be |             |
|             |             |             | changed   |             |
|             |             |             | by the    |             |
|             |             |             | given     |             |
|             |             |             | amount.   |             |
|             |             |             | Not       |             |
|             |             |             |           |             |
|             |             |             |  applicable |             |
|             |             |             | to all    |             |
|             |             |             | data      |             |
|             |             |             | effect    |             |
|             |             |             | subtypes. |             |
|             |             |             |           |             |
|             |             |             | ●         |             |
|             |             |             | **        |             |
|             |             |             | *Assign***: |             |
|             |             |             | Replaces  |             |
|             |             |             | value by  |             |
|             |             |             | *amount*. |             |
|             |             |             |           |             |
|             |             |             | ●         |             |
|             |             |             | ***A      |             |
|             |             |             | bsolute***: |             |
|             |             |             | Adds      |             |
|             |             |             | *amount*  |             |
|             |             |             | to        |             |
|             |             |             |           |             |
|             |             |             |  attribute. |             |
|             |             |             |           |             |
|             |             |             | ●         |             |
|             |             |             | ***       |             |
|             |             |             | Percent***: |             |
|             |             |             |           |             |
|             |             |             |  Multiplies |             |
|             |             |             | attribute |             |
|             |             |             | value by  |             |
|             |             |             | *amount*. |             |
|             |             |             |           |             |
|             |             |             | ●         |             |
|             |             |             | ***Base   |             |
|             |             |             | Percent***: |             |
|             |             |             | Adjusts\  |             |
|             |             |             | attribute |             |
|             |             |             | value by  |             |
|             |             |             | *amount*, |             |
|             |             |             | using the |             |
|             |             |             | original  |             |
|             |             |             | unaltered |             |
|             |             |             | attribute |             |
|             |             |             | value as  |             |
|             |             |             | base.     |             |
|             |             |             |           |             |
|             |             |             | ●         |             |
|             |             |             | ***O      |             |
|             |             |             | verride***: |             |
|             |             |             | Replaces  |             |
|             |             |             | *both*    |             |
|             |             |             | the       |             |
|             |             |             | current   |             |
|             |             |             | and the   |             |
|             |             |             | original  |             |
|             |             |             | (base)    |             |
|             |             |             | attribute |             |
|             |             |             | value by  |             |
+=============+=============+=============+=============+=============+
+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+
