+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| **pattern**                     | Defined as child node.          |
|                                   |                                 |
|                                   | Determines core data for unit   |
|                                   | spawning.                       |
+===================================+===================================+
| **type**                          | Pattern type. Can be set to     |
|                                   | *simple* or *leaving*.          |
|                                   |                                 |
|                                   | No special handling exists for\ |
|                                   | pattern types other than        |
|                                   | *leaving*, which allows the     |
|                                   | *offset* value to be used for   |
|                                   | determining position unit will  |
|                                   | move to when spawned.           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| **quantity**                      | Unit amount.                    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+
|             |             | **offset**  | Defined   |             |
|             |             |             | as        |             |
|             |             |             | sub-child |             |
|             |             |             | node of\  |             |
|             |             |             |           |             |
|             |             |             |  *Pattern*. |             |
|             |             |             | When      |             |
|             |             |             | pattern   |             |
|             |             |             | type is   |             |
|             |             |             | set to    |             |
|             |             |             |           |             |
|             |             |             |  *leaving*, |             |
|             |             |             | defines   |             |
|             |             |             | offset to |             |
|             |             |             | be        |             |
|             |             |             | applied   |             |
|             |             |             | for       |             |
|             |             |             |           |             |
|             |             |             | determining |             |
|             |             |             | position  |             |
|             |             |             | unit will |             |
|             |             |             | move to   |             |
|             |             |             | once      |             |
|             |             |             | created.  |             |
|             |             |             |             |             |
|             |             |             | Ignored     |             |
|             |             |             | when a      |             |
|             |             |             | gather      |             |
|             |             |             | point is    |             |
|             |             |             | set.        |             |
+=============+=============+=============+=============+=============+
+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+

70

**Data Effect Target**

+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **Attribute**         | **Description**       | **Syntax**            |
+=======================+=======================+=======================+
| **type**              | Sets target type    | \<Effect            |
|                       | for data effect.    | type=\'Data\'       |
|                       | Can take the        |                     |
|                       | following values:\  |  subtype=\'GodPower\' |
|                       | ● ***player***:     |                     |
|                       | Affects             |  power=\'ForestFire\' |
|                       |                     | amount=\'1.0\'      |
|                       |  player/civilization\ | cooldown=\'180\'    |
|                       | data.               | relat               |
|                       |                     | ivity=\'Absolute\'\>\ |
|                       | ● ***tech*:**       | \<Target            |
|                       | Affects data for a  | type=\'Player\'/\>\ |
|                       | given technology.   | \</Effect\        |
|                       |                     |                     |
|                       | ● ***techAll*:**    | \<Effect            |
|                       | Affects data for    | type=\'Data\'       |
|                       | all technologies.   | amount=\'0.75\'     |
|                       |                     | subtype=\'cost\'    |
|                       | ●                   | resource=\'Food\'   |
|                       | ***techWithFlag*:** | rela                |
|                       | Affects data for    | tivity=\'Percent\'\>\ |
|                       | all technologies    | \<Target            |
|                       | having a specific   | type=\'Tech\'\>He   |
|                       | tech flag set.      | avyCavalry\</Target\|
|                       |                     | \</Effect\        |
|                       | ● ***techType*:**   |                     |
|                       | Affects data for    | \<Effect            |
|                       | all\                | type=\'Data\'       |
|                       | technologies of a   | amount=\'0.25\'     |
|                       | specific tech type. | subty               |
|                       |                     | pe=\'ResearchPoints\' |
|                       | ● ***protoUnit*:**  | rela                |
|                       | Affects data for    | tivity=\'Percent\'\>\ |
|                       | all\                | \<Target            |
|                       | protoUnits          | ty                  |
|                       | belonging to the    | pe=\'techType\'\>Hero |
|                       | provided unitType.  | Promotion\</Target\>\ |
|                       | Multiple unit types | \</Effect\        |
|                       | can be provided by  |                       |
|                       | separating them     |                       |
|                       | with \|.            |                       |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **ignoreNature**      | If present,         | \<Effect            |
|                       | prevents effect     | type=\'Data\'       |
|                       | from being applied  | amount=\'0.50\'     |
|                       | if current player   |                     |
|                       | is Nature/Gaia.     | subtype=\'Hitpoints\' |
|                       |                       | relativi            |
|                       |                       | ty=\'BasePercent\'\>\ |
|                       |                       | \<Target            |
|                       |                       | type=\'ProtoUnit\'  |
|                       |                       | ignoreNature=       |
|                       |                       | \'\'\>Unit\</Target\|
|                       |                       | \</Effect\        |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **ignoreAgeUps**      | If present,         | \<Effect            |
|                       | technologies with   | type=\'Data\'       |
|                       | *AgeUpgrade* flag   | amount=\'0.50\'     |
|                       | set won't be        | subtype=\'Cost\'    |
|                       | affected by this    | resource=\'Food\'   |
|                       | effect. Only        | relativi            |
|                       | applicable if       | ty=\'BasePercent\'\>\ |
|                       | *type* is set to    | \<Target            |
|                       | *techAll*.          | type=\'techAll\'    |
|                       |                       | ignoreAgeUps=\'\'\  |
|                       |                       | excludeTypes        |
|                       |                       | =\'HeroPromotion\|Res |
|                       |                       | earchableCommand\'/\|
|                       |                       | \</Effect\        |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **excludeTypes**      | Sets tech types to  |                       |
|                       | be excluded from    |                       |
|                       | this effect,        |                       |
|                       | separated by \|,    |                       |
|                       | commas or space.    |                       |
|                       | Only applicable if  |                       |
|                       | *type* is set to    |                       |
|                       | *techAll*.          |                       |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+

|             | next unit |             |             |             |
|             | to be     |             |             |             |
|             | spawned.  |             |             |             |
+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+
|             |             |             | **contri    | Defines   |
|             |             |             | butorType** | expected  |
|             |             |             |             |           |
|             |             |             |             | contributor |
|             |             |             |             | type. Can |
|             |             |             |             | be set to |
|             |             |             |             | *Unit*    |
|             |             |             |             | for       |
|             |             |             |             | (*Damage* |
|             |             |             |             | and       |
|             |             |             |             | *         |
|             |             |             |             | DeathCount* |
|             |             |             |             | goals) or |
|             |             |             |             |           |
|             |             |             |             |  *Resource* |
|             |             |             |             | (for      |
|             |             |             |             |           |
|             |             |             |             |  *Resource* |
|             |             |             |             | goals).   |
+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+
|             |             |             | **cont    | C         |
|             |             |             | ributorID** | ontributor. |
|             |             |             |             | Should be |
|             |             |             |             | set to    |
|             |             |             |             | attacker  |
|             |             |             |             | unit type |
|             |             |             |             | or lost   |
|             |             |             |             | unit type |
|             |             |             |             | for       |
|             |             |             |             | *Damage*  |
|             |             |             |             | or        |
|             |             |             |             | *         |
|             |             |             |             | DeathCount* |
|             |             |             |             | goals,    |
|             |             |             |             | re        |
|             |             |             |             | spectively, |
|             |             |             |             | or        |
|             |             |             |             | resource  |
|             |             |             |             | type for  |
|             |             |             |             |           |
|             |             |             |             |  *Resource* |
|             |             |             |             | goals.    |
+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+

**Appendix**

+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **Supported KBStats   |                       |                       |
| for Tech Effects**    |                       |                       |
+=======================+=======================+=======================+
| **Name**              | **Parameter**         | **Description**       |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **enemyUnitsKilled**  | **-**                 | Enemy units killed  |
|                       |                       | by the current      |
|                       |                       | player.             |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **e                   | **-**                 | Enemy buildings     |
| nemyBuildingsKilled** |                       | destroyed by the    |
|                       |                       | current player.     |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **unitsLost**         | **-**                 | Units lost by the   |
|                       |                       | current player.     |
|                       |                       | Doesn't account for |
|                       |                       | deleted units.      |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **buildingsLost**     | **-**                 | Buildings lost by   |
|                       |                       | the current player. |
|                       |                       | Doesn't account for |
|                       |                       | deleted buildings.  |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **tradeProfit**       | Resource ID           | Total trade route   |
|                       |                       | income for the      |
|                       |                       | current player, for |
|                       |                       | either the given    |
|                       |                       | resource, if        |
|                       |                       | parameter is set,   |
|                       |                       | or all resources    |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **                    | **-**                 | Total amount of     |
| totalMinedResources** |                       | resources obtained  |
|                       |                       | from objects of     |
|                       |                       | type                |
|                       |                       | *MinedResource* or  |
|                       |                       | *LogicalTypeAccum   |
|                       |                       | ulateMinedResources*. |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **unitsKilledCost**   | **-**                 | Total cost of all   |
|                       |                       | units killed by the |
|                       |                       | current player;     |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **                    | **-**                 | Total cost of all   |
| buildingsKilledCost** |                       | buildings destroyed |
|                       |                       | by the current      |
|                       |                       | player;             |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **villagersLost**     | **-**                 | Total amount of     |
|                       |                       | villagers (i.e.     |
|                       |                       | units of            |
|                       |                       | *Lo                 |
|                       |                       | gicalTypeLandEconomy* |
|                       |                       | unitType) lost by   |
|                       |                       | the player.         |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **herdablesLost**     | **-**                 | Total amount of     |
|                       |                       | herdables lost by   |
|                       |                       | the player.         |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **totalTechCost**     | Resource ID           | Total cost of all   |
|                       |                       | technologies        |
|                       |                       | researched by the   |
|                       |                       | player.             |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **costUnitsTrained**  | Resource ID           | Total cost of all   |
|                       |                       | units trained by    |
|                       |                       | the player.         |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
| **researchCount**     | **-**                 | Total number of     |
|                       |                       | technologies        |
|                       |                       | researched by the   |
|                       |                       | player.             |
+-----------------------+-----------------------+-----------------------+
